proc sql;
create table all as
selct * from work2 as aa
left join mike.n3adult as bb
on aa.seqn=bb.seqn;
quit;

proc freq data=all;
tables har1;
run;

data mike.n3;
set all;
run;


proc sql;
create table one as
select * from demo9900 as cc
left join exam9900 as dd
on cc.seqn=dd.seqn;
quit;

proc sql;
create table two as
select * from one as ee
left join smoke9900 as ff
on ee.seqn=ff.seqn;
quit;

proc sql;
create table three as
select * from two as gg
left join haq9900 as hh
on gg.seqn=hh.seqn;
quit;

proc sql;
create table four as
select * from three as jj
left join alcohol9900 as kk
on jj.seqn=kk.seqn;
quit;

proc sql;
create table five as
select * from four as ll
left join htn9900 as mm
on ll.seqn=mm.seqn;
quit;

proc sql;
create table six as 
select * from five as nn
left join dm9900 as oo
on nn.seqn=oo.seqn;
quit;

proc sql;
create table seven as
select * from six as pp
left join medical9900 as qq
on pp.seqn=qq.seqn;
quit;

data mike.n9900;
set seven;
run;

proc sql;
create table all3 as
select * from mike.n3 as y3
left join nhanes_III as z3
on y3.seqn=z3.seqn;
quit;

data mike.n3_mort;
set all3;
run;

data n3statin;
set n3med;
where hqrxcode=1664 or hqrxcode=3064 or hqrxcode=3088;
run;
data n3statin2;
set n3statin;
keep seqn hqrxcode;
run;
proc sort data=n3statin2;
by seqn;
run;
data n3first;
set n3statin2;
by seqn;
if first.seqn then output;
run;

proc sql;
create table n3aa as
select * from mike.n3_mort as u2
left join n3first as mm2
on u2.seqn=mm2.seqn;
quit;

data mike.n3_mort_med;
set n3aa;
run;



proc freq data=rx1112;
tables rxddrug;
run;

data statin1112;
set rx1112;
if rxddrug='ATORVASTATIN' or rxddrug='LOVASTATIN' or rxddrug='PITAVASTATIN' or rxddrug='PRAVASTATIN' or rxddrug='ROSUVASTATIN'
or rxddrug='SIMVASTATIN';
run;
proc sort data=statin1112;
by seqn;
run;
data s1112;
set statin1112;
by seqn;
if first.seqn then output;
run;
data s1112a;
set s1112;
keep seqn rxddrug;
run;

proc sql;
create table stat11 as
select * from mike.n1112_mort2 as yes1
left join s1112a as no1
on yes1.seqn=no1.seqn;
quit;
data mike.n1112_mort2_med;
set stat11;
run;

if rxddrug='ATORVASTATIN' or rxddrug='LOVASTATIN' or rxddrug='PITAVASTATIN' or rxddrug='PRAVASTATIN' or rxddrug='ROSUVASTATIN'
or rxddrug='SIMVASTATIN';
run;

by seqn;
run;
data s0910;
set statin0910;
by seqn;
if first.seqn then output;
run;
data s0910a;
set s0910;

or rxd240b='SIMVASTATIN';

proc contents data=mike.n3_mort_med;
run;

proc sql;
create table mike.addlab as
select * from mike.n3_mort_med as b
left join mike.n3_labkeep as c
on b.seqn=c.seqn;
quit;

proc means data=mike.addlab n nmiss mean min max;
var sCr ldl hba1c haza11ar haza11br;
run;




data mike.nhanes3_step1;
set mike.addlab;
if hsageu=2 then age=hsageir;
else if hsageu=1 then age=hsageir/12;

if hssex=1 then male=1;
else if hssex=2 then male=0;

if (dmaethnr=1 or dmaethnr=2) then race=3;
else if (dmaethnr=3) and dmaracer=1 then race=1;
else if (dmaethnr=3) and dmaracer=2 then race=2;
else if (dmaethnr=3) and dmaracer=3 then race=4;

rename hshsizer=householdsize;

if hfa8r ge 0 and hfa8r lt 9 then edlevel=1;
else if hfa8r ge 9 and hfa8r lt 12 then edlevel=2;
else if hfa8r=12 then edlevel=3;
else if hfa8r gt 12 and hfa8r lt 16 then edlevel=4;
else if hfa8r=16 or hfa8r=17 then edlevel=5;
else if hfa8r=88 or hfa8r=99 or hfa8r=. then edlevel=.;

if dmppir lt 12.0 then poverty_ratio=dmppir;
else if dmppir gt 12.0 then poverty_ratio=.;

if hfa12=1 or hfa12=2 then married=1;
else if hfa12 ge 3 and hfa12 lt 10 then married=0;
else if hfa12=88 or hfa12=99 or hfa12=. then married=.;

if hfd10r=1 or hfd10r=2 or hfd10r=3 or hfd10r=4 or hfd10r=5 or hfd10r=6 or hfd10r=7 or hfd10r=8 then occupa=1;
else if hfd10r=9 or hfd10r=10 or hfd10r=11 or hfd10r=12 or hfd10r=13 or hfd10r=14 or hfd10r=15 
or hfd10r=16 then occupa=2;
else if hfd10r=17 or hfd10r=18 or hfd10r=19 or hfd10r=20 or hfd10r=21 or hfd10r=22 or hfd10r=23 
or hfd10r=24 then occupa=3;
else if hfd10r=25 or hfd10r=26 or hfd10r=27 or hfd10r=28 or hfd10r=29 or hfd10r=30 or hfd10r=31 
or hfd10r=32 or hfd10r=33 or hfd10r=34 or hfd10r=35 or hfd10r=36 or hfd10r=37 or hfd10r=38 
or hfd10r=39 or hfd10r=40 then occupa=4;
else if hfd10r=88 or hfd10r=99 or hfd10r=. then occupa=.;

if hff7=1 then nofood=1;
else if hff7=2 then nofood=0;
else if hff7=8 or hff7=. then nofood=.;

if hab1=1 then genhealth=1;
else if hab1=2 then genhealth=2;
else if hab1=3 then genhealth=3;
else if hab1=4 then genhealth=4;
else if hab1=5 then genhealth=5;
else if hab1=8 or hab1=9 or hab1=. then genhealth=.;

if hac1c=1 then chf=1;
else if hac1c=2 then chf=0;
else if hac1c=8 or hac1c=9 or hac1c=. then chf=.;

if hac1d=1 then cva=1;
else if hac1d=2 then cva=0;
else if hac1d=8 or hac1d=9 or hac1d=. then cva=.;

if hac1e=1 then asthma=1;
else if hac1e=2 then asthma=0;
else if hac1e=8 or hac1e=9 or hac1e=. then asthma=.;

if hac1f=1 then bronch=1;
else if hac1f=2 then bronch=0;
else if hac1f=8 or hac1f=9 or hac1f=. then bronch=.;

if hac1g=1 then emph=1;
else if hac1g=2 then emph=0;
else if hac1g=8 or hac1g=9 or hac1g=. then emph=.;

if hac1o=1 then cancer=1;
else if hac1o=2 then cancer=0;
else if hac1o=8 or hac1o=9 or hac1o=. then cancer=.;

if had1=1 then dm_sr=1;
else if had1=2 then dm_sr=0;
else if had1=8 or had1=9 or had1=. then dm_sr=.;

if hae2=1 then htn_sr=1;
else if hae2=2 then htn_sr=0;
else if hae2=8 or hae2=9 or hae2=. then htn_sr=.;

if hae7=1 then chol_sr=1;
else if hae7=2 then chol_sr=0;
else if hae7=8 or hae7=9 or hae7=. then chol_sr=.;

if hae9d=1 then chol_med=1;
else if hae9d=2 then chol_med=0;
else if hae9d=8 or hae9d=9 or hae9d=. then chol_med=.;

if haf10=1 then ami=1;
else if haf10=2 then ami=0;
else if haf10=8 or haf10=9 or haf10=. then ami=.;

if had6=1 then insulin=1;
else if had6=2 then insulin=0;
else if had6=8 or had6=. then insulin=.;

if had10=1 then oralhypo=1;
else if had10=2 then oralhypo=0;
else if had10=8 or had10=9 or had10=. then oralhypo=.;

if hah1=1 then f_walk025mi=1;
else if hah1=2 then f_walk025mi=2;
else if hah1=3 then f_walk025mi=3;
else if hah1=4 then f_walk025mi=4;
else if hah1=8 or hah1=9 or hah1=. then f_walk025mi=.;

if hah2=1 then f_walk10=1;
else if hah2=2 then f_walk10=2;
else if hah2=3 then f_walk10=3;
else if hah2=4 then f_walk10=4;
else if hah2=8 or hah2=9 or hah2=. then f_walk10=.;

if hah3=1 then f_stoop=1;
else if hah3=2 then f_stoop=2;
else if hah3=3 then f_stoop=3;
else if hah3=4 then f_stoop=4;
else if hah3=8 or hah3=9 or hah3=. then f_stoop=.;

if hah4=1 then f_lift10=1;
else if hah4=2 then f_lift10=2;
else if hah4=3 then f_lift10=3;
else if hah4=4 then f_lift10=4;
else if hah4=8 or hah4=9 or hah4=. then f_lift10=.;

if hah5=1 then f_housework=1;
else if hah5=2 then f_housework=2;
else if hah5=3 then f_housework=3;
else if hah5=4 then f_housework=4;
else if hah5=8 or hah5=9 or hah5=. then f_housework=.;

if hah6=1 then f_meals=1;
else if hah6=2 then f_meals=2;
else if hah6=3 then f_meals=3;
else if hah6=4 then f_meals=4;
else if hah6=8 or hah6=9 or hah6=. then f_meals=.;

if hah7=1 then f_money=1;
else if hah7=2 then f_money=2;
else if hah7=3 then f_money=3;
else if hah7=4 then f_money=4;
else if hah7=8 or hah7=9 or hah7=. then f_money=.;

if hah8=1 then f_walkrooms=1;
else if hah8=2 then f_walkrooms=2;
else if hah8=3 then f_walkrooms=3;
else if hah8=4 then f_walkrooms=4;
else if hah8=8 or hah8=9 or hah8=. then f_walkrooms=.;

if hah9=1 then f_stand=1;
else if hah9=2 then f_stand=2;
else if hah9=3 then f_stand=3;
else if hah9=4 then f_stand=4;
else if hah9=8 or hah9=9 or hah9=. then f_stand=.;

if hah10=1 then f_oob=1;
else if hah10=2 then f_oob=2;
else if hah10=3 then f_oob=3;
else if hah10=4 then f_oob=4;
else if hah10=8 or hah10=9 or hah10=. then f_oob=.;

if hah11=1 then f_eat=1;
else if hah11=2 then f_eat=2;
else if hah11=3 then f_eat=3;
else if hah11=4 then f_eat=4;
else if hah11=8 or hah11=9 or hah11=. then f_eat=.;

if hah12=1 then f_dress=1;
else if hah12=2 then f_dress=2;
else if hah12=3 then f_dress=3;
else if hah12=4 then f_dress=4;
else if hah12=8 or hah12=9 or hah12=. then f_dress=.;

dmi=bmpbmi*1;
dwt=bmpwt*1;
dht=bmpht*1;
dwaist=bmpwaist*1;

if har1=1 then ever_smoker=1;
else if har1=2 then ever_smoker=0;
else if har1=. or har1=8 then ever_smoker=.;

if har2 gt 0 and har2 lt 888 then age_smoke_start=har2;
else if har2 ge 888 or har2=0 or har2=. then age_smoke_start=.;

if har3=1 then smk_curr=1;
else if har3=2 or har1=2 then smk_curr=0;
else if har3=8 or har3=. then smk_curr=.;

if har3=2 or har1=2 or (har4s ge 1 and har4s lt 20) or har4s=666 or har4s=777 then smk_1ppd=0;
else if har4s ge 20 and har4s le 665 then smk_1ppd=1;
else if har4s=888 or har4s=999 or har4s=. then smk_1ppd=.;

if har5 lt 777 then smk_years=har5;
else if har5=777 then smk_years=1;
else if har5=888 or har5=999 or har5=. then smk_years=.;

if har11r lt 888 then age_quit=har11r;
else if har11r=888 or har11r=999 or har11r=. then age_quit=.;

if mape1=1 then ever_drinker=1;
else if mape1=2 then ever_drinker=0;
else if mape1=8 or mape1=9 or mape1=. then ever_drinker=.;

if mape1=1 and mape2=1 then curr_drinker=1;
else if mape1=2 or (mape1=1 and mape2=2) then curr_drinker=0;
else if mape2=8 or mape2=9 or mape2=. then curr_drinker=.;

if mape3s=0 or (mape3s=. and mape2=2) or (mape3s=. and mape1=2) then alcohol_days=0; 
else if mape3s gt 0 and mape3s lt 888 then alcohol_days=mape3s;
else if mape3s=888 or mape3s=999 or mape3s=. then alcohol_days=.;

if mape3s=0 or (mape3s=. and mape2=2) or (mape3s=. and mape1=2) or mape6s=0 then binge_pastyr=0;
else if mape6s gt 0 and mape6s le 365 then binge_pastyr=1;
else if mape6s=888 or mape6s=999 or (mape3s ne . and mape6s=.) then binge_pastyr=.;

if mape7=1 then binge_ever=1;
else if mape7=2 or (mape1=2 and mape7=.) then binge_ever=0;
else if mape7=8 or mape7=9 or (mape1 ne 2 and mape7=.) then binge_ever=.;

rename sdppsu6=psu6;
rename sdpstra6=stratum6;

if haza11ar ge 0 and haza11ar lt 300 then sbp=haza11ar;
else if haza11ar lt 0 or haza11ar ge 300 or haza11ar=. then sbp=.;

if haza11br ge 0 and haza11br lt 300 then dbp=haza11br;
else if haza11br lt 0 or haza11br ge 300 or haza11br=. then dbp=.;

sCr7=((0.96*sCr)-0.184)/0.7;
sCr9=((0.96*sCr)-0.184)/0.9;
run;

/* sCr adjusted for method  AJKD 2007;50:918 */


data mike.nhanes3_step2;
set mike.nhanes3_step1;
sCr7_a=sCr7**-0.241;
sCr7_b=sCr7**-1.2;
sCr9_c=sCr9**-0.302;
sCr9_d=sCr9**-1.2;
eage=0.9938**age;
run;

proc print data=mike.nhanes3_step2 (obs=10);
var scr7 scr7_a scr7_b scr9_c scr9_d;
run;

data mike.nhanes3_step2;
set mike.nhanes3_step2;
if male=0 and (sCr ne . and sCr le 0.7) then egfr=142*scr7_a*eage*1.012;
else if male=0 and (sCr ne . and sCr gt 0.7) then egfr=142*scr7_b*eage*1.012;
else if male=1 and (sCr ne . and sCr le 0.9) then egfr=142*scr9_c*eage;
else if male=1 and (sCr ne . and sCr gt 0.9) then egfr=142*scr9_d*eage;
else if scr=. then egfr=.;
run;

proc print data=mike.nhanes3_step2 (obs=10);
var male scr scr7 scr7_a scr7_b scr9_c scr9_d age eage egfr ;
run;

proc freq data=mike.nhanes3_step2 nlevels;
tables seqn/noprint;
run;

data mike.nhanes3_step3;
set mike.nhanes3_step2;
if egfr ne . and egfr lt 60.0 then ckd=1;
else if egfr ne . and egfr ge 60.0 then ckd=0;
else if egfr=. then ckd=.;

if (hba1c ne . and hba1c ge 6.5) or (dm_sr=1 and (insulin=1 or oralhypo=1)) then diab=1;
else if ((hba1c ne . and hba1c lt 6.5) and dm_sr=0) or (hba1c=. and dm_sr=0) then diab=0;
else if hba1c=. and dm_sr=. then diab=.;

if (sbp ne . and sbp ge 130) or (dbp ne . and dbp ge 80) or hae5a=1 then highbp=1;
else if (sbp ne . and sbp lt 130) and (dbp ne . and dbp lt 80) and (hae5a=2 or hae5a=8 or hae5a=9 or hae5a=.) then highbp=0;
else highbp=.;

if (chol_sr=1 and chol_med=1) or ((ami=1 or cva=1 or dm_sr=1) and ldl ge 100) or ((ami=0 and cva=0 and dm_sr=0) and ldl ge 220) then
hyperlipid=1;
else if (chol_sr=0 or chol_med=0) or ((ami=1 or cva=1 or dm_sr=1) and (ldl ne . and ldl lt 100)) or ((ami=0 and cva=0 and dm_sr=0) and (ldl 
ne . and ldl lt 220)) then
hyperlipid=0;
else if (chol_sr=. or chol_med=.) and ldl=. then hyperlipid=.;
run;



proc print data=mike.nhanes3_step3 (obs=40);
var chol_sr chol_med ami cva dm_sr ldl hyperlipid;
run;


data mike.nhanes3_step4;
set mike.nhanes3_step3;
if dmi lt 100 then bmi=dmi;
else if dmi ge 100 or dmi=. then bmi=.;
if dwt lt 1000 then wt=dwt;
else if dwt ge 1000 or dwt=. then wt=.;
if dht lt 1000 then ht=dht;
else if dht ge 1000 or dht=. then ht=.;
if dwaist lt 1000 then waist=dwaist;
else if dwaist ge 1000 or dwaist=. then waist=.;

if smk_curr=1 and smk_1ppd=1 then smoke_4cat=1;
else if (smk_curr=1 and smk_1ppd=0) or (smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (age-age_quit lt 2.0)) then smoke_4cat=2;
else if smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (age-age_quit ge 2.0) then smoke_4cat=3;
else if ever_smoker=0 then smoke_4cat=4;
else if ever_smoker=. or smk_curr=. then smoke_4cat=.;

if smk_curr=1 then smoke_3cat_strict=1;
else if smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 then smoke_3cat_strict=2;
else if ever_smoker=0 then smoke_3cat_strict=3;
else if ever_smoker=. or smk_curr=. then smoke_3cat_strict=.;

if smk_curr=1 or (smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (age-age_quit lt 2.0)) then smoke_3cat=1;
else if (smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (age-age_quit ge 2.0)) then smoke_3cat=2;
else if ever_smoker=0 then smoke_3cat=3;
else if ever_smoker=. or smk_curr=. then smoke_3cat=.;

if mape1 ne . and alcohol_days=0 then alcohol_cat=0;
else if mape1 ne . and (alcohol_days ge 1 and alcohol_days le 365) and binge_pastyr=0 then alcohol_cat=1;
else if mape1 ne . and (alcohol_days ge 1 and alcohol_days le 365) and binge_pastyr=1 then alcohol_cat=2;
else if mape1=. then alcohol_cat=.;

if hqrxcode ne . then statin=1;
else if hqrxcode=. then statin=0;

if bronch=1 or emph=1 then copd=1;
else if bronch=0 and emph=0 then copd=0;
else if bronch=. and emph=. then copd=.;
run;


proc freq data=mike.nhanes3_step4;
tables ever_smoker smk_curr smk_1ppd smoke_4cat smoke_3cat_strict
smoke_3cat mape1 alcohol_days alcohol_cat binge_pastyr ucod_leading bronch emph copd;
run;

 
data mike.nhanes3_step5;
set mike.nhanes3_step4;
keep seqn wtpfex6 wtpfhx6 dmpstat sdpphase psu6 stratum6 wtpfex1 wtpfhx1
wtpfex2 wtpfhx2 age male race householdsize edlevel poverty_ratio married genhealth
chf cva asthma bronch emph cancer hac3os dm_sr htn_sr chol_sr chol_med ami f_walk025mi f_walk10 f_stoop f_lift10
f_housework f_meals f_money f_walkrooms f_stand f_oob f_eat f_dress bmi wt ht waist 
ever_smoker age_smoke_start smk_curr smk_1ppd smk_years age_quit ever_drinker curr_drinker alcohol_days
binge_pastyr binge_ever eligstat mortstat ucod_leading permth_int permth_exm alcohol_cat smoke_4cat 
smoke_3cat_strict smoke_3cat statin insulin oralhypo sbp dbp highbp diab hba1c ldl hyperlipid egfr ckd copd;

data n99a;
set n99;

if smk_curr=1 and smk_1ppd=1 then smoke_4cat=1;
else if (smk_curr=1 and smk_1ppd=0) or (smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (yrs_quit lt 2.0)) then smoke_4cat=2;
else if smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (yrs_quit ge 2.0) then smoke_4cat=3;
else if ever_smoker=0 then smoke_4cat=4;
else if ever_smoker=. or smk_curr=. then smoke_4cat=.;

if smk_curr=1 and (smk_1ppd=1 or smk_1ppd=.) then smoke_4cat_imphigh=1;
else if (smk_curr=1 and smk_1ppd=0) or (smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (yrs_quit lt 2.0)) then smoke_4cat_imphigh=2;
else if smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (yrs_quit ge 2.0) then smoke_4cat_imphigh=3;
else if ever_smoker=0 then smoke_4cat_imphigh=4;
else if ever_smoker=. or smk_curr=. then smoke_4cat_imphigh=.;

if smk_curr=1 and smk_1ppd=1 then smoke_4cat_implow=1;
else if (smk_curr=1 and (smk_1ppd=. or smk_1ppd=0)) or (smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (yrs_quit lt 2.0)) then smoke_4cat_implow=2;
else if smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (yrs_quit ge 2.0) then smoke_4cat_implow=3;
else if ever_smoker=0 then smoke_4cat_implow=4;
else if ever_smoker=. or smk_curr=. then smoke_4cat_implow=.;

if smk_curr=1 then smoke_3cat_strict=1;
else if smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 then smoke_3cat_strict=2;
else if ever_smoker=0 then smoke_3cat_strict=3;
else if ever_smoker=. or smk_curr=. then smoke_3cat_strict=.;

if smk_curr=1 or (smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and yrs_quit lt 2.0) then smoke_3cat=1;
else if (smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and yrs_quit ge 2.0) then smoke_3cat=2;
else if ever_smoker=0 then smoke_3cat=3;
else if ever_smoker=. or smk_curr=. then smoke_3cat=.;

if alq100 ne . and alcohol_days=0 then alcohol_cat=0;
else if alq100 ne . and (alcohol_days ge 1 and alcohol_days le 365) and binge_pastyr=0 then alcohol_cat=1;
else if alq100 ne . and (alcohol_days ge 1 and alcohol_days le 365) and binge_pastyr=1 then alcohol_cat=2;
else if alq100=. then alcohol_cat=.;

if rxd240b ne ' ' then statin=1;
else if rxd240b=' ' then statin=0;
run;

set n01;

if smk_curr=1 and smk_1ppd=1 then smoke_4cat=1;
else if (smk_curr=1 and smk_1ppd=0) or (smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (yrs_quit lt 2.0)) then smoke_4cat=2;
else if smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (yrs_quit ge 2.0) then smoke_4cat=3;
else if ever_smoker=0 then smoke_4cat=4;
else if ever_smoker=. or smk_curr=. then smoke_4cat=.;

if smk_curr=1 and (smk_1ppd=1 or smk_1ppd=.) then smoke_4cat_imphigh=1;
else if (smk_curr=1 and smk_1ppd=0) or (smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (yrs_quit lt 2.0)) then smoke_4cat_imphigh=2;
else if smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (yrs_quit ge 2.0) then smoke_4cat_imphigh=3;
else if ever_smoker=0 then smoke_4cat_imphigh=4;
else if ever_smoker=. or smk_curr=. then smoke_4cat_imphigh=.;

if smk_curr=1 and smk_1ppd=1 then smoke_4cat_implow=1;
else if (smk_curr=1 and (smk_1ppd=. or smk_1ppd=0)) or (smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (yrs_quit lt 2.0)) then smoke_4cat_implow=2;
else if smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (yrs_quit ge 2.0) then smoke_4cat_implow=3;
else if ever_smoker=0 then smoke_4cat_implow=4;
else if ever_smoker=. or smk_curr=. then smoke_4cat_implow=.;

if smk_curr=1 then smoke_3cat_strict=1;
else if smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 then smoke_3cat_strict=2;
else if ever_smoker=0 then smoke_3cat_strict=3;
else if ever_smoker=. or smk_curr=. then smoke_3cat_strict=.;

if smk_curr=1 or (smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and yrs_quit lt 2.0) then smoke_3cat=1;
else if (smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and yrs_quit ge 2.0) then smoke_3cat=2;
else if ever_smoker=0 then smoke_3cat=3;
else if ever_smoker=. or smk_curr=. then smoke_3cat=.;

if ald100 ne . and alcohol_days=0 then alcohol_cat=0;
else if ald100 ne . and (alcohol_days ge 1 and alcohol_days le 365) and binge_pastyr=0 then alcohol_cat=1;
else if ald100 ne . and (alcohol_days ge 1 and alcohol_days le 365) and binge_pastyr=1 then alcohol_cat=2;
else if ald100=. then alcohol_cat=.;


if rxd240b ne ' ' then statin=1;
else if rxd240b=' ' then statin=0;
run;


proc print data=n01a (obs=25);
var seqn smq020 ever_smoker smd030 age_smoke_start smq040 smk_curr smd070 smk_1ppd smd075 smk_years smq050q smq050u yrs_quit
smoke_4cat smoke_4cat_imphigh smoke_4cat_implow smoke_3cat;
run;
proc print data=n01a (obs=100);
var seqn ever_smoker smk_curr smk_1ppd smq050q smq050u yrs_quit
smoke_4cat smoke_4cat_imphigh smoke_4cat_implow smoke_3cat smoke_3cat_strict;
run;

proc freq data=n01a;
tables smq020 ever_smoker smd030 age_smoke_start smq040 smk_curr smd070 smk_1ppd smd075 smk_years smd055 yrs_quit
smoke_4cat smoke_4cat_imphigh smoke_4cat_implow smoke_3cat smoke_3cat_strict rxd240b statin;
run;


proc print data=n01a (obs=50);
var seqn age ald100 alq110 alq120q alq140q alq150 binge_ever alcohol_days binge_pastyr alcohol_cat ;
run;
proc freq data=n01a;
tables binge_pastyr alcohol_cat rxd240b statin;
run;

proc freq data=n01a;
tables male race edlevel dmdeduc2 married dmdmartl race ridreth2 genhealth;
run;

data mike.nhanes0102_keep;
set n01a;
keep seqn psu stratum wtmec2yr age male race householdsize edlevel poverty_ratio married genhealth
chf cva asthma bronch emph cancer mcq230a dm htn chol ami 
f_walk025mi f_walk10 f_stoop f_lift10 f_housework f_meals f_money f_walkrooms f_stand f_oob f_eat f_dress 
bmi wt ht waist 
ever_smoker age_smoke_start smk_curr smk_1ppd smk_years yrs_quit ever_drinker alcohol_days
binge_pastyr binge_ever eligstat mortstat ucod_leading permth_int permth_exm alcohol_cat smoke_4cat 
smoke_4cat_imphigh smoke_4cat_implow smoke_3cat_strict smoke_3cat statin;
run;


/* end */



/* Nhanes 2009 - 2012 */
/* import labs and bp measurements */


data bp;
set mike.bp09;
sbp=mean(bpxsy1,bpxsy2,bpxsy3);
dbp=mean(bpxdi1,bpxdi2,bpxdi3);
run;

proc print data=bp (obs=20);
run;

data bp1;
set bp;
keep seqn sbp dbp;
run;

proc sql;
create table intro as
select * from mike.n0910_mort2_med as d
left join bp1 as e
on d.seqn=e.seqn;
quit;

proc sql;
create table intro2 as
select * from intro as g
left join mike.pf09 as h
on g.seqn=h.seqn;
quit;

proc contents data=intro2;
run;

data mike.nhanes09_step1;
set intro2;
rename ridageyr=age;
if riagendr=1 then male=1;
else if riagendr=2 then male=0;
if ridreth1=3 then race=1;
else if ridreth1=4 then race=2;
else if ridreth1=1 or ridreth1=2 then race=3;
else if ridreth1=5 then race=4;
rename dmdhhsiz=householdsize;

if dmdeduc2=1 then edlevel=1;
else if dmdeduc2=2 then edlevel=2;
else if dmdeduc2=3 then edlevel=3;
else if dmdeduc2=4 then edlevel=4;
else if dmdeduc2=5 then edlevel=5;
else if dmdeduc2=7 or dmdeduc2=9 or dmdeduc2=. then edlevel=.;

if indfmpir ne . then poverty_ratio=indfmpir;
else if indfmpir=. then poverty_ratio=.;

if dmdmartl=1 then married=1;
else if dmdmartl ge 1 and dmdmartl lt 77 then married=0;
else if dmdmartl=77 or dmdmartl=99 or dmdmartl=. then married=.;

if huq010=1 then genhealth=1;
else if huq010=2 then genhealth=2;
else if huq010=3 then genhealth=3;
else if huq010=4 then genhealth=4;
else if huq010=5 then genhealth=5;
else if huq010=7 or huq010=9 or huq010=. then genhealth=.;

if mcq160b=1 then chf=1;
else if mcq160b=2 then chf=0;
else if mcq160b=7 or mcq160b=9 or mcq160b=. then chf=.;

if mcq160f=1 then cva=1;
else if mcq160f=2 then cva=0;
else if mcq160f=7 or mcq160f=9 or mcq160f=. then cva=.;

if mcq010=1 then asthma=1;
else if mcq010=2 then asthma=0;
else if mcq010 or mcq010=9 or mcq010=. then asthma=.;

if mcq160k=1 then bronch=1;
else if mcq160k=2 then bronch=0;
else if mcq160k=7 or mcq160k=9 or mcq160k=. then bronch=.;

if mcq160g=1 then emph=1;
else if mcq160g=2 then emph=0;
else if mcq160g=7 or mcq160g=9 or mcq160g=. then emph=.;

if mcq220=1 and (mcq230a ne 32 and mcq230a ne 33) then cancer=1;
else if mcq220=2 or (mcq220=1 and (mcq230a=32 or mcq230a=33)) then cancer=0;
else if mcq220=9 or mcq220=. then cancer=.;

if diq010=1 then dm_sr=1;
else if diq010=2 or diq010=3 then dm_sr=0;
else if diq010=7 or diq010=9 or diq010=. then dm_sr=.;

if diq050=1 then insulin=1;
else if diq050=2 then insulin=0;
else if diq050=7 or diq050=9 or diq050=. then insulin=.;

if diq070=1 then oralhypo=1;
else if diq070=2 then oralhypo=0;
else if diq070=7 or diq070=9 or diq070=. then oralhypo=.;


 if bpq020=1 then htn_sr=1;
else if bpq020=2 then htn_sr=0;
else if bpq020=7 or bpq020=9 or bpq020=. then htn_sr=.;

if bpq050a=1 then bp_med=1;
else if bpq050a=2 then bp_med=0;
else if bpq050a=7 or bpq050a=9 or bpq050a=. then bp_med=.;

 if bpq080=1 then chol_sr=1;
else if bpq080=2 then chol_sr=0;
else if bpq080=7 or bpq080=9 or bpq080=. then chol_sr=.;

if bpq100d=1 then chol_med=1;
else if bpq100d=2 then chol_med=0;
else if bpq100d=7 or bpq100d=9 or bpq100d=. then chol_med=.;

if mcq160e=1 then ami=1;
else if mcq160e=2 then ami=0;
else if mcq160e=7 or mcq160e=9 or mcq160e=. then ami=.;

if pfq061b=1 then f_walk025mi=1;
else if pfq061b=2 then f_walk025mi=2;
else if pfq061b=3 then f_walk025mi=3;
else if pfq061b=4 then f_walk025mi=4;
else if pfq061b=7 or pfq061b=9 or pfq061b=. then f_walk025mi=.;

if pfq061c=1 then f_walk10=1;
else if pfq061c=2 then f_walk10=2;
else if pfq061c=3 then f_walk10=3;
else if pfq061c=4 then f_walk10=4;
else if pfq061c=7 or pfq061c=9 or pfq061c=. then f_walk10=.;

if pfq061d=1 then f_stoop=1;
else if pfq061d=2 then f_stoop=2;
else if pfq061d=3 then f_stoop=3;
else if pfq061d=4 then f_stoop=4;
else if pfq061d=7 or pfq061d=9 or pfq061d=. then f_stoop=.;

if pfq061e=1 then f_lift10=1;
else if pfq061e=2 then f_lift10=2;
else if pfq061e=3 then f_lift10=3;
else if pfq061e=4 then f_lift10=4;
else if pfq061e=7 or pfq061e=9 or pfq061e=. then f_lift10=.;

if pfq061f=1 then f_housework=1;
else if pfq061f=2 then f_housework=2;
else if pfq061f=3 then f_housework=3;
else if pfq061f=4 then f_housework=4;
else if pfq061f=7 or pfq061f=9 or pfq061f=. then f_housework=.;

if pfq061g=1 then f_meals=1;
else if pfq061g=2 then f_meals=2;
else if pfq061g=3 then f_meals=3;
else if pfq061g=4 then f_meals=4;
else if pfq061g=7 or pfq061g=9 or pfq061g=. then f_meals=.;

if pfq061a=1 then f_money=1;
else if pfq061a=2 then f_money=2;
else if pfq061a=3 then f_money=3;
else if pfq061a=4 then f_money=4;
else if pfq061a=7 or pfq061a=9 or pfq061a=. then f_money=.;

if pfq061h=1 then f_walkrooms=1;
else if pfq061h=2 then f_walkrooms=2;
else if pfq061h=3 then f_walkrooms=3;
else if pfq061h=4 then f_walkrooms=4;
else if pfq061h=7 or pfq061h=9 or pfq061h=. then f_walkrooms=.;

if pfq061d=1 then f_stoop=1;
else if pfq061d=2 then f_stoop=2;
else if pfq061d=3 then f_stoop=3;
else if pfq061d=4 then f_stoop=4;
else if pfq061d=7 or pfq061d=9 or pfq061d=. then f_stoop=.;

if pfq061i=1 then f_stand=1;
else if pfq061i=2 then f_stand=2;
else if pfq061i=3 then f_stand=3;
else if pfq061i=4 then f_stand=4;
else if pfq061i=7 or pfq061i=9 or pfq061i=. then f_stand=.;

if pfq061j=1 then f_oob=1;
else if pfq061j=2 then f_oob=2;
else if pfq061j=3 then f_oob=3;
else if pfq061j=4 then f_oob=4;
else if pfq061j=7 or pfq061j=9 or pfq061j=. then f_oob=.;

if pfq061k=1 then f_eat=1;
else if pfq061k=2 then f_eat=2;
else if pfq061k=3 then f_eat=3;
else if pfq061k=4 then f_eat=4;
else if pfq061k=7 or pfq061k=9 or pfq061k=. then f_eat=.;

if pfq061l=1 then f_dress=1;
else if pfq061l=2 then f_dress=2;
else if pfq061l=3 then f_dress=3;
else if pfq061l=4 then f_dress=4;
else if pfq061l=7 or pfq061l=9 or pfq061l=. then f_dress=.;

rename bmxbmi=bmi;
rename bmxwt=wt;
rename bmxht=ht;
rename bmxwaist=waist;

if smq020=1 then ever_smoker=1;
else if smq020=2 then ever_smoker=0;
else if smq020=7 or smq020=9 or smq020=. then ever_smoker=.;

if smd030 gt 0 and smd030 lt 777 then age_smoke_start=smd030;
else if smd030=0 or smd030=999 or smd030=777 or smd030=. then age_smoke_start=.;

if smq040=1 or smq040=2 then smk_curr=1;
else if smq040=3 or smq020=2 then smk_curr=0;
else if smq040=7 or smq040=8 or smq040=. then smk_curr=.;

if smq040=3 or smq020=2 or (smd650 ge 1 and smd650 lt 20) then smk_1ppd=0;
else if smd650 ge 20 and smd650 lt 777 then smk_1ppd=1;
else if smd650=777 or smd650=999 or smd650=. then smk_1ppd=.;

if (smd030 ge 5 and smd030 le 80) and (smd055 ge 3 and smd055 le 80) then
smk_years=smd055-smd030;
else smk_years=.;

if smq050u=4 then yrs_quit=smq050q;
else if smq050u=3 then yrs_quit=smq050q/12;
else if smq050u=2 or smq050u=1 then yrs_quit=smq050q/52;
else if smq050u=7 or smq050u=9 or smq050u=. then yrs_quit=.;



if alq110=1 or alq101=1 then ever_drinker=1;
else if alq110=2 then ever_drinker=0;
else if alq110=7 or alq110=9 or alq110=. or alq101=9 or alq101=. then ever_drinker=.;

if alq120q=0 or (alq120q=. and alq110=2) then alcohol_days=0;
else if (alq120q ge 1 and alq120q le 365) and alq120u=1 then alcohol_days=alq120q*52;
else if (alq120q ge 1 and alq120q le 365) and alq120u=2 then alcohol_days=alq120q*12;
else if (alq120q ge 1 and alq120q le 365) and alq120u=3 then alcohol_days=alq120q;
else if alq120q=777 or alq120q=999 or alq120q=. then alcohol_days=.;

if alq120q=0 or alq140q=0 or (alq120q=. and alq110=2) then binge_pastyr=0;
else if (alq140q ge 1 and alq140q le 365) then binge_pastyr=1;
else if (alq140q=999 or alq140q=777 or alq140q=.) then binge_pastyr=.;


if alq150=1 then binge_ever=1;
else if alq150=2 or alq110=2 then binge_ever=0;
else if alq150=. or alq150=9 or alq150=7 then binge_ever=.;

run;


data cr;
set mike.cr09;
keep seqn lbxscr;
run;
data hg;
set mike.hg09;
keep seqn lbxgh;
run;
data chol;
set mike.chol09;
keep seqn lbdldl;
run;

data cr1;
set cr;
rename lbxscr=sCr;
run;
data cr1;
set cr1;
sCr7=sCr/0.7;
sCr9=sCr/0.9;
run;
data hg1;
set hg;
rename lbxgh=hba1c;
run;
data chol1;
set chol;
rename lbdldl=ldl;
run;


proc sql;
create table yost as
select * from mike.nhanes09_step1 as y
left join cr1 as z
on y.seqn=z.seqn
left join hg1 as u
on y.seqn=u.seqn
left join chol1 as v
on y.seqn=v.seqn;
quit;

proc print data=yost (obs=10);
var seqn ever_smoker dm_sr sbp dbp sCr sCr7 sCr9 hba1c ldl insulin oralhypo;
run;






data mike.nhanes09_step2;
set yost;
sCr7_a=sCr7**-0.241;
sCr7_b=sCr7**-1.2;
sCr9_c=sCr9**-0.302;
sCr9_d=sCr9**-1.2;
eage=0.9938**age;
run;

proc print data=mike.nhanes09_step2 (obs=10);
var scr7 scr7_a scr7_b scr9_c scr9_d;
run;

data mike.nhanes09_step2;
set mike.nhanes09_step2;
if male=0 and (sCr ne . and sCr le 0.7) then egfr=142*scr7_a*eage*1.012;
else if male=0 and (sCr ne . and sCr gt 0.7) then egfr=142*scr7_b*eage*1.012;
else if male=1 and (sCr ne . and sCr le 0.9) then egfr=142*scr9_c*eage;
else if male=1 and (sCr ne . and sCr gt 0.9) then egfr=142*scr9_d*eage;
else if scr=. then egfr=.;
run;

proc print data=mike.nhanes09_step2 (obs=10);
var male scr scr7 scr7_a scr7_b scr9_c scr9_d age eage egfr ;
run;


data mike.nhanes09_step3;
set mike.nhanes09_step2;
if egfr ne . and egfr lt 60.0 then ckd=1;
else if egfr ne . and egfr ge 60.0 then ckd=0;
else if egfr=. then ckd=.;

if (hba1c ne . and hba1c ge 6.5) or (dm_sr=1 and (insulin=1 or oralhypo=1)) then diab=1;
else if ((hba1c ne . and hba1c lt 6.5) and dm_sr=0) or (hba1c=. and dm_sr=0) then diab=0;
else if hba1c=. and dm_sr=. then diab=.;

if (sbp ne . and sbp ge 130) or (dbp ne . and dbp ge 80) or bp_med=1 then highbp=1;
else if (sbp ne . and sbp lt 130) and (dbp ne . and dbp lt 80) and (bp_med=0 or bp_med=.) then highbp=0;
else highbp=.;

if (chol_sr=1 and chol_med=1) or ((ami=1 or cva=1 or dm_sr=1) and ldl ge 100) or ((ami=0 and cva=0 and dm_sr=0) and ldl ge 220) then
hyperlipid=1;
else if (chol_sr=0 or chol_med=0) or ((ami=1 or cva=1 or dm_sr=1) and (ldl ne . and ldl lt 100)) or ((ami=0 and cva=0 and dm_sr=0) and (ldl 
ne . and ldl lt 220)) then
hyperlipid=0;
else if (chol_sr=. or chol_med=.) and ldl=. then hyperlipid=.;
run;



proc print data=mike.nhanes09_step3 (obs=40);
var alq101 alq110 alq120q alq120u alq140q alq150 ever_drinker alcohol_days binge_pastyr binge_ever;
run;



proc print data=mike.nhanes09_step3 (obs=40);
var chol_sr chol_med ami cva dm_sr insulin oralhypo hba1c diab ldl hyperlipid;
run;

proc freq data=mike.nhanes09_step3;
tables dm_sr*(insulin oralhypo);
run;

data mike.nhanes09_step4;
set mike.nhanes09_step3;
rename wtmec2yr=weight2y;
rename sdmvpsu=psu;
rename sdmvstra=stratum;

if smk_curr=1 and smk_1ppd=1 then smoke_4cat=1;
else if (smk_curr=1 and smk_1ppd=0) or (smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (yrs_quit lt 2.0)) then smoke_4cat=2;
else if smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (yrs_quit ge 2.0) then smoke_4cat=3;
else if ever_smoker=0 then smoke_4cat=4;
else if ever_smoker=. or smk_curr=. then smoke_4cat=.;

if smk_curr=1 then smoke_3cat_strict=1;
else if smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 then smoke_3cat_strict=2;
else if ever_smoker=0 then smoke_3cat_strict=3;
else if ever_smoker=. or smk_curr=. then smoke_3cat_strict=.;

if smk_curr=1 or (smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (yrs_quit lt 2.0)) then smoke_3cat=1;
else if (smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (yrs_quit ge 2.0)) then smoke_3cat=2;
else if ever_smoker=0 then smoke_3cat=3;
else if ever_smoker=. or smk_curr=. then smoke_3cat=.;

if alcohol_days=0 then alcohol_cat=0;
else if (alcohol_days ge 1 and alcohol_days le 365) and binge_pastyr=0 then alcohol_cat=1;
else if (alcohol_days ge 1 and alcohol_days le 365) and binge_pastyr=1 then alcohol_cat=2;
else if alcohol_days=. then alcohol_cat=.;


if rxddrug ne ' ' then statin=1;
else if rxddrug=' ' then statin=0;

if bronch=1 or emph=1 then copd=1;
else if bronch=0 and emph=0 then copd=0;
else if bronch=. and emph=. then copd=.;
run;


proc freq data=mike.nhanes09_step4;
tables ever_smoker smk_curr smk_1ppd smoke_4cat smoke_3cat_strict
smoke_3cat alcohol_days alcohol_cat binge_pastyr ucod_leading copd bronch emph;
run;


 
data mike.nhanes09_step5;
set mike.nhanes09_step4;
keep seqn weight2y psu stratum age male race householdsize edlevel poverty_ratio married genhealth
chf cva asthma bronch emph cancer mcq230a dm_sr htn_sr chol_sr chol_med ami f_walk025mi f_walk10 f_stoop f_lift10
f_housework f_meals f_money f_walkrooms f_stand f_oob f_eat f_dress bmi wt ht waist 
ever_smoker age_smoke_start smk_curr smk_1ppd smk_years yrs_quit ever_drinker alcohol_days
binge_pastyr binge_ever eligstat mortstat ucod_leading permth_int permth_exm alcohol_cat smoke_4cat 
smoke_3cat_strict smoke_3cat statin insulin oralhypo sbp dbp highbp diab hba1c ldl hyperlipid egfr ckd copd;
run;










/* Nhanes 2011 - 2012 */
/* import labs and bp measurements */


data bp;
set mike.bp11;
sbp=mean(bpxsy1,bpxsy2,bpxsy3);
dbp=mean(bpxdi1,bpxdi2,bpxdi3);
run;

proc print data=bp (obs=20);
run;

data bp1;
set bp;
keep seqn sbp dbp;
run;

proc sql;
create table concl as 
select * from mike.n1112_mort2_med as d
left join bp1 as e
on d.seqn=e.seqn;
quit;




data mike.nhanes11_step1;
set concl;
rename ridageyr=age;
if riagendr=1 then male=1;
else if riagendr=2 then male=0;
if ridreth1=3 then race=1;
else if ridreth1=4 then race=2;
else if ridreth1=1 or ridreth1=2 then race=3;
else if ridreth1=5 then race=4;
rename dmdhhsiz=householdsize;

if dmdeduc2=1 then edlevel=1;
else if dmdeduc2=2 then edlevel=2;
else if dmdeduc2=3 then edlevel=3;
else if dmdeduc2=4 then edlevel=4;
else if dmdeduc2=5 then edlevel=5;
else if dmdeduc2=7 or dmdeduc2=9 or dmdeduc2=. then edlevel=.;

if indfmpir ne . then poverty_ratio=indfmpir;
else if indfmpir=. then poverty_ratio=.;

if dmdmartl=1 then married=1;
else if dmdmartl ge 1 and dmdmartl lt 77 then married=0;
else if dmdmartl=77 or dmdmartl=99 or dmdmartl=. then married=.;

if huq010=1 then genhealth=1;
else if huq010=2 then genhealth=2;
else if huq010=3 then genhealth=3;
else if huq010=4 then genhealth=4;
else if huq010=5 then genhealth=5;
else if huq010=7 or huq010=9 or huq010=. then genhealth=.;

if mcq160b=1 then chf=1;
else if mcq160b=2 then chf=0;
else if mcq160b=7 or mcq160b=9 or mcq160b=. then chf=.;

if mcq160f=1 then cva=1;
else if mcq160f=2 then cva=0;
else if mcq160f=7 or mcq160f=9 or mcq160f=. then cva=.;

if mcq010=1 then asthma=1;
else if mcq010=2 then asthma=0;
else if mcq010 or mcq010=9 or mcq010=. then asthma=.;

if mcq160k=1 then bronch=1;
else if mcq160k=2 then bronch=0;
else if mcq160k=7 or mcq160k=9 or mcq160k=. then bronch=.;

if mcq160g=1 then emph=1;
else if mcq160g=2 then emph=0;
else if mcq160g=7 or mcq160g=9 or mcq160g=. then emph=.;

if mcq220=1 and (mcq230a ne 32 and mcq230a ne 33) then cancer=1;
else if mcq220=2 or (mcq220=1 and (mcq230a=32 or mcq230a=33)) then cancer=0;
else if mcq220=9 or mcq220=. then cancer=.;

if diq010=1 then dm_sr=1;
else if diq010=2 or diq010=3 then dm_sr=0;
else if diq010=7 or diq010=9 or diq010=. then dm_sr=.;

if diq050=1 then insulin=1;
else if diq050=2 then insulin=0;
else if diq050=7 or diq050=9 or diq050=. then insulin=.;

if diq070=1 then oralhypo=1;
else if diq070=2 then oralhypo=0;
else if diq070=7 or diq070=9 or diq070=. then oralhypo=.;


 if bpq020=1 then htn_sr=1;
else if bpq020=2 then htn_sr=0;
else if bpq020=7 or bpq020=9 or bpq020=. then htn_sr=.;

if bpq050a=1 then bp_med=1;
else if bpq050a=2 then bp_med=0;
else if bpq050a=7 or bpq050a=9 or bpq050a=. then bp_med=.;

 if bpq080=1 then chol_sr=1;
else if bpq080=2 then chol_sr=0;
else if bpq080=7 or bpq080=9 or bpq080=. then chol_sr=.;

if bpq100d=1 then chol_med=1;
else if bpq100d=2 then chol_med=0;
else if bpq100d=7 or bpq100d=9 or bpq100d=. then chol_med=.;

if mcq160e=1 then ami=1;
else if mcq160e=2 then ami=0;
else if mcq160e=7 or mcq160e=9 or mcq160e=. then ami=.;

if pfq061b=1 then f_walk025mi=1;
else if pfq061b=2 then f_walk025mi=2;
else if pfq061b=3 then f_walk025mi=3;
else if pfq061b=4 then f_walk025mi=4;
else if pfq061b=7 or pfq061b=9 or pfq061b=. then f_walk025mi=.;

else if pfq061c=2 then f_walk10=2;
else if pfq061c=3 then f_walk10=3;
else if pfq061c=4 then f_walk10=4;
else if pfq061c=7 or pfq061c=9 or pfq061c=. then f_walk10=.;

if pfq061d=1 then f_stoop=1;
else if pfq061d=2 then f_stoop=2;
else if pfq061d=3 then f_stoop=3;
else if pfq061d=4 then f_stoop=4;
else if pfq061d=7 or pfq061d=9 or pfq061d=. then f_stoop=.;

if pfq061e=1 then f_lift10=1;
else if pfq061e=2 then f_lift10=2;
else if pfq061e=3 then f_lift10=3;
else if pfq061e=4 then f_lift10=4;
else if pfq061e=7 or pfq061e=9 or pfq061e=. then f_lift10=.;

if pfq061f=1 then f_housework=1;
else if pfq061f=2 then f_housework=2;
else if pfq061f=3 then f_housework=3;
else if pfq061f=4 then f_housework=4;
else if pfq061f=7 or pfq061f=9 or pfq061f=. then f_housework=.;

if pfq061g=1 then f_meals=1;
else if pfq061g=2 then f_meals=2;
else if pfq061g=3 then f_meals=3;
else if pfq061g=4 then f_meals=4;
else if pfq061g=7 or pfq061g=9 or pfq061g=. then f_meals=.;

if pfq061a=1 then f_money=1;
else if pfq061a=2 then f_money=2;
else if pfq061a=3 then f_money=3;
else if pfq061a=4 then f_money=4;
else if pfq061a=7 or pfq061a=9 or pfq061a=. then f_money=.;

if pfq061h=1 then f_walkrooms=1;
else if pfq061h=2 then f_walkrooms=2;
else if pfq061h=3 then f_walkrooms=3;
else if pfq061h=4 then f_walkrooms=4;
else if pfq061h=7 or pfq061h=9 or pfq061h=. then f_walkrooms=.;

if pfq061d=1 then f_stoop=1;
else if pfq061d=2 then f_stoop=2;
else if pfq061d=3 then f_stoop=3;
else if pfq061d=4 then f_stoop=4;
else if pfq061d=7 or pfq061d=9 or pfq061d=. then f_stoop=.;

if pfq061i=1 then f_stand=1;
else if pfq061i=2 then f_stand=2;
else if pfq061i=3 then f_stand=3;
else if pfq061i=4 then f_stand=4;
else if pfq061i=7 or pfq061i=9 or pfq061i=. then f_stand=.;

if pfq061j=1 then f_oob=1;
else if pfq061j=2 then f_oob=2;
else if pfq061j=3 then f_oob=3;
else if pfq061j=4 then f_oob=4;
else if pfq061j=7 or pfq061j=9 or pfq061j=. then f_oob=.;

if pfq061k=1 then f_eat=1;
else if pfq061k=2 then f_eat=2;
else if pfq061k=3 then f_eat=3;
else if pfq061k=4 then f_eat=4;
else if pfq061k=7 or pfq061k=9 or pfq061k=. then f_eat=.;

if pfq061l=1 then f_dress=1;
else if pfq061l=2 then f_dress=2;
else if pfq061l=3 then f_dress=3;
else if pfq061l=4 then f_dress=4;
else if pfq061l=7 or pfq061l=9 or pfq061l=. then f_dress=.;

rename bmxbmi=bmi;
rename bmxwt=wt;
rename bmxht=ht;
rename bmxwaist=waist;

if smq020=1 then ever_smoker=1;
else if smq020=2 then ever_smoker=0;
else if smq020=7 or smq020=9 or smq020=. then ever_smoker=.;

if smd030 gt 0 and smd030 lt 777 then age_smoke_start=smd030;
else if smd030=0 or smd030=999 or smd030=777 or smd030=. then age_smoke_start=.;

if smq040=1 or smq040=2 then smk_curr=1;
else if smq040=3 or smq020=2 then smk_curr=0;
else if smq040=7 or smq040=8 or smq040=. then smk_curr=.;

if smq040=3 or smq020=2 or (smd650 ge 1 and smd650 lt 20) then smk_1ppd=0;
else if smd650 ge 20 and smd650 lt 777 then smk_1ppd=1;
else if smd650=777 or smd650=999 or smd650=. then smk_1ppd=.;

if (smd030 ge 5 and smd030 le 80) and (smd055 ge 3 and smd055 le 80) then
smk_years=smd055-smd030;
else smk_years=.;

if smq050u=4 then yrs_quit=smq050q;
else if smq050u=3 then yrs_quit=smq050q/12;
else if smq050u=2 or smq050u=1 then yrs_quit=smq050q/52;
else if smq050u=7 or smq050u=9 or smq050u=. then yrs_quit=.;



if alq110=1 or alq101=1 then ever_drinker=1;
else if alq110=2 then ever_drinker=0;
else if alq110=7 or alq110=9 or alq110=. or alq101=9 or alq101=. then ever_drinker=.;

if alq120q=0 or (alq120q=. and alq110=2) then alcohol_days=0;
else if (alq120q ge 1 and alq120q le 365) and alq120u=1 then alcohol_days=alq120q*52;
else if (alq120q ge 1 and alq120q le 365) and alq120u=2 then alcohol_days=alq120q*12;
else if (alq120q ge 1 and alq120q le 365) and alq120u=3 then alcohol_days=alq120q;
else if alq120q=777 or alq120q=999 or alq120q=. then alcohol_days=.;

if alq120q=0 or alq141q=0 or (alq120q=. and alq110=2) then binge_pastyr=0;
else if (alq141q ge 1 and alq141q le 365) then binge_pastyr=1;
else if (alq141q=999 or alq141q=777 or alq141q=.) then binge_pastyr=.;


if alq151=1 then binge_ever=1;
else if alq151=2 or alq110=2 then binge_ever=0;
else if alq151=. or alq151=9 or alq151=7 then binge_ever=.;

run;



proc print data=mike.nhanes11_step1 (obs=50);
var smq020 ever_smoker smd030 age_smoke_start smq040 smk_curr smd650 smk_1ppd smd055 smk_years age
smq050q smq050u yrs_quit ;
run;
proc print data=mike.nhanes11_step1 (obs=50);
var alq110 alq101 ever_drinker alq120q alcohol_days alq141q binge_pastyr alq151 binge_ever;
run;




data cr;
set mike.cr11;
keep seqn lbxscr;
run;
data hg;
set mike.hgb11;
keep seqn lbxgh;
run;
data chol;
set mike.chol11;
keep seqn lbdldl;
run;

data cr1;
set cr;
rename lbxscr=sCr;
run;
data cr1;
set cr1;
sCr7=sCr/0.7;
sCr9=sCr/0.9;
run;
data hg1;
set hg;
rename lbxgh=hba1c;
run;
data chol1;
set chol;
rename lbdldl=ldl;
run;


proc sql;
create table sost as
select * from mike.nhanes11_step1 as w
left join cr1 as t
on w.seqn=t.seqn
left join hg1 as r
on w.seqn=r.seqn
left join chol1 as s
on w.seqn=s.seqn;
quit;

proc print data=sost (obs=10);
var seqn ever_smoker dm_sr sbp dbp sCr sCr7 sCr9 hba1c ldl insulin oralhypo;
run;



data mike.nhanes11_step2;
set sost;
sCr7_a=sCr7**-0.241;
sCr7_b=sCr7**-1.2;
sCr9_c=sCr9**-0.302;
sCr9_d=sCr9**-1.2;
eage=0.9938**age;
run;

proc print data=mike.nhanes11_step2 (obs=10);
var scr7 scr7_a scr7_b scr9_c scr9_d;
run;

data mike.nhanes11_step2;
set mike.nhanes11_step2;
if male=0 and (sCr ne . and sCr le 0.7) then egfr=142*scr7_a*eage*1.012;
else if male=0 and (sCr ne . and sCr gt 0.7) then egfr=142*scr7_b*eage*1.012;
else if male=1 and (sCr ne . and sCr le 0.9) then egfr=142*scr9_c*eage;
else if male=1 and (sCr ne . and sCr gt 0.9) then egfr=142*scr9_d*eage;
else if scr=. then egfr=.;
run;

proc print data=mike.nhanes11_step2 (obs=10);
var male scr scr7 scr7_a scr7_b scr9_c scr9_d age eage egfr ;
run;




data mike.nhanes11_step3;
set mike.nhanes11_step2;
if egfr ne . and egfr lt 60.0 then ckd=1;
else if egfr ne . and egfr ge 60.0 then ckd=0;
else if egfr=. then ckd=.;

if (hba1c ne . and hba1c ge 6.5) or (dm_sr=1 and (insulin=1 or oralhypo=1)) then diab=1;
else if ((hba1c ne . and hba1c lt 6.5) and dm_sr=0) or (hba1c=. and dm_sr=0) then diab=0;
else if hba1c=. and dm_sr=. then diab=.;

if (sbp ne . and sbp ge 130) or (dbp ne . and dbp ge 80) or bp_med=1 then highbp=1;
else if (sbp ne . and sbp lt 130) and (dbp ne . and dbp lt 80) and (bp_med=0 or bp_med=.) then highbp=0;
else highbp=.;

if (chol_sr=1 and chol_med=1) or ((ami=1 or cva=1 or dm_sr=1) and ldl ge 100) or ((ami=0 and cva=0 and dm_sr=0) and ldl ge 220) then
hyperlipid=1;
else if (chol_sr=0 or chol_med=0) or ((ami=1 or cva=1 or dm_sr=1) and (ldl ne . and ldl lt 100)) or ((ami=0 and cva=0 and dm_sr=0) and (ldl 
ne . and ldl lt 220)) then
hyperlipid=0;
else if (chol_sr=. or chol_med=.) and ldl=. then hyperlipid=.;
run;



proc print data=mike.nhanes11_step3 (obs=40);
var alq101 alq110 alq120q alq120u alq141q alq151 ever_drinker alcohol_days binge_pastyr binge_ever;
run;



proc print data=mike.nhanes11_step3 (obs=40);
var chol_sr chol_med ami cva dm_sr insulin oralhypo hba1c diab ldl hyperlipid;
run;




data mike.nhanes11_step4;
set mike.nhanes11_step3;
rename wtmec2yr=weight2y;
rename sdmvpsu=psu;
rename sdmvstra=stratum;

if smk_curr=1 and smk_1ppd=1 then smoke_4cat=1;
else if (smk_curr=1 and smk_1ppd=0) or (smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (yrs_quit lt 2.0)) then smoke_4cat=2;
else if smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (yrs_quit ge 2.0) then smoke_4cat=3;
else if ever_smoker=0 then smoke_4cat=4;
else if ever_smoker=. or smk_curr=. then smoke_4cat=.;

if smk_curr=1 then smoke_3cat_strict=1;
else if smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 then smoke_3cat_strict=2;
else if ever_smoker=0 then smoke_3cat_strict=3;
else if ever_smoker=. or smk_curr=. then smoke_3cat_strict=.;

if smk_curr=1 or (smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (yrs_quit lt 2.0)) then smoke_3cat=1;
else if (smk_curr=0 and ever_smoker=1 and (yrs_quit ge 2.0)) then smoke_3cat=2;
else if ever_smoker=0 then smoke_3cat=3;
else if ever_smoker=. or smk_curr=. then smoke_3cat=.;

if alcohol_days=0 then alcohol_cat=0;
else if (alcohol_days ge 1 and alcohol_days le 365) and binge_pastyr=0 then alcohol_cat=1;
else if (alcohol_days ge 1 and alcohol_days le 365) and binge_pastyr=1 then alcohol_cat=2;
else if alcohol_days=. then alcohol_cat=.;


if rxddrug ne ' ' then statin=1;
else if rxddrug=' ' then statin=0;

if bronch=1 or emph=1 then copd=1;
else if bronch=0 and emph=0 then copd=0;
else if bronch=. and emph=. then copd=.;
run;


proc freq data=mike.nhanes11_step4;
tables ever_smoker smk_curr smk_1ppd smoke_4cat smoke_3cat_strict
smoke_3cat alcohol_days alcohol_cat binge_pastyr ucod_leading copd bronch emph;
run;


 
data mike.nhanes11_step5;
set mike.nhanes11_step4;
keep seqn weight2y psu stratum age male race householdsize edlevel poverty_ratio married genhealth
chf cva asthma bronch emph cancer mcq230a dm_sr htn_sr chol_sr chol_med ami f_walk025mi f_walk10 f_stoop f_lift10
f_housework f_meals f_money f_walkrooms f_stand f_oob f_eat f_dress bmi wt ht waist 
ever_smoker age_smoke_start smk_curr smk_1ppd smk_years yrs_quit ever_drinker alcohol_days
binge_pastyr binge_ever eligstat mortstat ucod_leading permth_int permth_exm alcohol_cat smoke_4cat 
smoke_3cat_strict smoke_3cat statin insulin oralhypo sbp dbp highbp diab hba1c ldl hyperlipid egfr ckd copd;
run;
